The `addAlertMigrations()` function creates the legacy `alert` table with fields like dashboard_id, panel_id, name, message, settings, and state. This table represents dashboard-level alerts that were tied to specific dashboard panels. The legacy API storage layer is implemented in `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go` through the `legacyStorage` struct, which provides REST API access to these legacy alert rules by delegating to the provisioning service.\\n\\n## Unified Alert Rule Storage and Engine\\nThe unified alerting (ngalert) engine replaces the legacy system with a new architecture:\\n\\n1. **Data Model**: `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` defines the `AlertRule` struct that represents the new alert rule format with enhanced features including rule groups, expressions, and flexible notification settings.\\n\\n2. **Storage**: `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` implements the `DBstore` struct providing database operations for alert rules including `InsertAlertRules()`, `GetAlertRuleByUID()`, `UpdateAlertRules()`, and `ListAlertRules()`.\\n\\n3. **Main Service**: `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` contains the `AlertNG` struct which is the primary unified alerting service initialized through `ProvideService()` function. The `FixEarlyMigration()` function handles early ng-alerting configurations, while `AddDashboardUIDPanelIDMigration()` migrates dashboard and panel references from annotations.
